(As of late 2024, Firefly is integrated into apps like Photoshop, Illustrator, Adobe Express, etc., with credits to meter-heavy usage.) 若超出包含的信用額，可透過套裝購買更多信用（而較高階的訂閱者則有較大的或無限的信用額）。對於企業用戶，Adobe 可能會將 Firefly AI 整合至現有授權中，並採用基於用量的定價方式。(截至 2024 年底，Firefly 已整合至如 Photoshop、Illustrator、Adobe Express 等應用中，並以信用點來計量使用量。)

    Canva (Magic Studio) – Canva is a graphic design platform popular for social media graphics, presentations, posters, etc., and it has infused AI across its tools. Canva (Magic Studio) – Canva 是一個廣受歡迎的圖形設計平台，常用於社交媒體圖文、簡報、海報等，並已在其工具中融入 AI 功能。

    Canva’s Magic Write is an AI text generator for coming up with copy (e.g., social captions or brainstorm lists)​, Magic Design can auto-generate slide or design layouts from a prompt or image, and Text-to-Image (powered by Stable Diffusion) lets users generate custom images within Canva. It also offers AI image editing (e.g., Magic Eraser to remove objects). Canva 的 Magic Write 是用來生成文字內容的 AI 工具（例如社交媒體標語或創意清單）​，Magic Design 則可根據提示或圖片自動生成簡報或設計版面，而文字轉圖片（由 Stable Diffusion 提供支援）則讓用戶能在 Canva 內生成客製化圖片。它也提供 AI 圖片編輯功能（例如 Magic Eraser 可移除圖片中的物件）。

    Features: ease of use – AI suggestions appear in the same simple interface; integration with Canva’s vast template library. 功能：使用方便 – AI 提示會出現在相同的簡潔介面；與 Canva 廣泛的模板庫整合。

    Pricing: Canva’s core features include a free tier. AI features like Magic Write are free but limited (free users can use Magic Write up to 25 times in total)​. To unlock more, users need Canva Pro (~$12.99/month for individuals) – Pro users get significantly higher AI usage (Magic Write up to 75 queries per month​, and other AI tools without heavy limit). 價格：Canva 的核心功能包含免費版。AI 功能如 Magic Write 是免費但有限制（免費用戶總共只能使用 Magic Write 25 次）。要解鎖更多功能，用戶需要 Canva Pro（個人約 $12.99/月）– Pro 用戶可獲得顯著更高的 AI 使用次數（Magic Write 每月最多可使用 75 次，其他 AI 工具則無嚴格限制）。

    Canva for Teams (starts ~$14.99/month for five users) also includes the AI features. In summary, Canvas AI is included in Pro subscriptions; the free plan allows some experimentation, but regular use requires Pro. Canva for Teams（五人起約 $14.99/月）也包含 AI 功能。總結來說，Canvas AI 納入在 Pro 訂閱中；免費方案允許一些實驗，但日常使用則需要 Pro。

    Runway ML – (Experimental/creative)  An AI toolkit for creators, known for its video editing AI. Runway’s Gen-2 model can create AI-generated videos from text prompts or reference images (an emerging capability) and perform video edits (like background removal and motion tracking with AI). It also has image generation and editing similar to Stable Diffusion. Runway ML –（實驗性/創意性）為創作者提供的 AI 工具組，以視頻編輯 AI 著稱。Runway 的 Gen-2 模型可以從文字提示或參考圖片生成 AI 創作視頻（一種新興功能），並執行視頻編輯（如背景去除、使用 AI 進行動態追蹤）。它也擁有類似 Stable Diffusion 的圖片生成與編輯功能。

    Pricing: Runway ML has a free tier with limited credits. Paid plans start at around $12/month for more generation minutes and scale up for pro usage. (This tool is more niche for video professionals and researchers but is notable as a cutting-edge creative AI.) 定價：Runway ML 提供免費層，包含有限的信用額。付費方案從每月約 $12 開始，提供更多的生成分鐘數，並根據專業用途逐步升級。(此工具較適合影片專業人士與研究者，但作為一項最先進的創意 AI 工具，仍具備特色。)

    1. Productivity and Office AI Tools
    2. 效率與辦公室 AI 工具

    Grammarly – A widely-used AI writing assistant that helps with spelling, grammar, clarity, and style in documents, emails, and online writing. Grammarly goes beyond basic spellcheck by offering suggestions to rephrase sentences for conciseness or tone (e.g., making a sentence sound more professional or friendly). Grammarly – 一個廣為使用的 AI 寫作助手，協助改善文件、電子郵件及線上寫作的拼寫、語法、清晰度與風格。Grammarly 不僅僅是基本的拼寫檢查，還能提供建議，協助重新表述句子以達到更簡潔或更合適的語氣（例如，使句子聽起來更專業或更親切）。

    It also includes a plagiarism checker for academic use and a generative AI feature (GrammarlyGO) that can draft or rewrite passages on demand​ . 它也包含一個用於學術用途的抄襲檢查功能，以及一個生成式 AI 特色功能（GrammarlyGO），可根據需求撰寫或重寫段落。

    Usage:  It works via browser extension, MS Office add-in, desktop app, or web editor – making it easy to integrate into daily writing tasks. 使用方式：透過瀏覽器擴充功能、MS Office 加入項、桌面應用程式或網頁編輯器運作，讓它輕鬆融入日常寫作任務中。

    Pricing: Grammarly has a Free tier with basic grammar and spelling checks. Premium (for individuals) costs about $12/month (billed annually at $144)​, unlocking advanced style suggestions, vocabulary enhancement, tone adjustments, and plagiarism detection. 價格：Grammarly 提供免費版，包含基本的語法與拼寫檢查。付費版（個人用）每月約 $12（年度計費 $144），可解鎖進階的風格建議、詞彙提升、語氣調整與抄襲檢測功能。

    Business (Teams) is around $15 per user/month (with centralized admin and style guides). (Grammarly often offers discounts for students and volume licenses. As noted, certain groups qualify for free access, e.g., some educational institutions have Grammarly campus licenses.)​ 企業版（Teams）則為每位使用者每月約 $15（包含集中式管理員與風格指南）。(Grammarly 通常會為學生與批量授權提供折扣。如前所述，某些群體可獲得免費使用資格，例如部分教育機構擁有 Grammarly 校園授權。)

    Notion AI – An AI assistant integrated into Notion (a popular workspace app for notes, wikis, and project management). Notion AI – 結合於 Notion（一個廣受歡迎的筆記、維基與專案管理工作空間應用程式）中的 AI 助手。

    Notion AI can generate content within any Notion page – for example; you can ask it to draft a blog outline, create a summary of meeting notes, or brainstorm ideas. Notion AI 可以在任何 Notion 頁面內產生內容 – 例如：你可以請它草擬部落格大綱、建立會議筆記摘要，或進行創意點子發想。

    It also can rewrite selected text (simplify language, change tone) and answer questions based on your workspace knowledge. 它也可以重新撰寫選定的文本（簡化語言、改變語氣），並根據你的工作空間知識來回答問題。

    Features: All functions occur in your Notion docs, streamlining workflows for writers and teams. Pricing: Notion AI is an add-on  to any Notion plan (including Free). It costs $10 per member/month as an add-on(with a 20% discount for annual billing)​. 功能：所有功能都在你的 Notion 文件中進行，為寫作者與團隊簡化工作流程。價格：Notion AI 是任何 Notion 計划（包括免費版）的附加功能。作為附加功能，每位成員每月需 $10，若以年度計費則有 20% 的折扣。

    Only one subscription is needed per workspace to give all members access​. (So if you have five users in Notion, enabling AI for all costs 5×$10 = $50/month on top of your base Notion plan. Education users get 50% off)​. Note:  Notion’s base software has Free, Plus ($8–$10), Business ($18) plans​. 每個工作空間只需一項訂閱，即可讓所有成員使用。 （因此，如果你的 Notion 有五位使用者，為所有使用者啟用 AI 功能，每月費用為 5×$10 = $50，加上你的基本 Notion 計划。教育使用者可享 50% 的折扣）​。注意：Notion 的基本軟體有 Free、Plus（$8–$10）、Business（$18）等計畫。

    A small team on Plus with AI would effectively pay ~$18–$22 per user for Notion+AI. 一個在 Plus 上擁有 AI 功能的小團隊，對 Notion+AI 的每位用戶收費約 ~$18–$22。

    Otter.ai – An AI meeting assistant that transcribes meetings and generates summaries in real-time. Otter.ai – 一個 AI 會議助理，可即時轉譯會議並產生摘要。

    Otter is commonly used in business and academia to record lectures, team meetings, interviews, and automatically get a written transcript (with speaker identification) and keyword highlights. Otter 常被用於商業與學術領域，用來錄製講座、團隊會議、訪談，並自動產生文字紀錄（含發言人識別）與關鍵字重點。

    Recent features include an AI Meeting Summary that produces a concise recap and action items shortly after the meeting ends. 近期新增的功能包括 AI 會議摘要，可在會議結束後不久產生簡明的回顧與行動事項。

    Usage: Works on web and mobile, and can integrate with Zoom or Microsoft Teams to automatically join and transcribe meetings. Pricing: There is a Basic free plan (transcribe 300 minutes/month, 30 min per conversation)​. Pro is $16.99/month (or ~$8.33/month annual) which provides 1,200 minutes/month, 90 min per conversation and some advanced export/search features​. Business is $30/user/month (or ~$20 if annual) and raises limits to 6,000 minutes, 4-hour meetings, plus team collaboration and live Zoom integration​. Enterprise plans with higher volumes and HIPAA compliance are available. (As of 2024, Otter’s Pro plan annual comes to $99/year, and Business $240/year/user​.)  The free tier is great for students and occasional use, while most business users opt for Pro or Business depending on organization size. 使用方式：支援網頁與行動裝置，並可整合 Zoom 或 Microsoft Teams 自動加入並轉譯會議。價格：有基本版的免費方案（每月可轉譯 300 分鐘，每場對話 30 分鐘）。Pro 版為每月 $16.99（或每年約 $8.33），提供每月 1,200 分鐘的轉譯時間，每場對話 90 分鐘，以及一些高階的匯出與搜尋功能。Business 版為每位使用者每月 $30（或每年約 $20），並提高使用上限至每月 6,000 分鐘、4 小時的會議，加上團隊協作與即時 Zoom 整合功能。亦有企業方案，提供更高使用量與 HIPAA 合規性。 (截至 2024 年，Otter 的 Pro 年付方案為 $99/年，Business 為 $240/年/使用者。) 免費方案很適合學生與偶爾使用的情況，而大多數企業使用者則會根據組織規模選擇 Pro 或 Business。

    Microsoft 365 Copilot – An AI assistant integrated into Microsoft’s Office 365 suite (Word, Excel, PowerPoint, Outlook, Teams). Copilot uses OpenAI GPT-4 to help users be more productive within these apps. For example, in Word it can draft documents based on prompts or data, in Excel it can analyze data and create formulas or summaries (“Tell me insights from this spreadsheet”), in PowerPoint it can generate slides from an outline, and in Outlook it can draft/reply to emails. In Teams, it can provide meeting summaries in real-time. Features: deeply integrated with the user’s files and context – it can pull relevant information from your calendar, emails, and documents to tailor its responses. Pricing: Microsoft 365 Copilot is an add-on for commercial Microsoft 365 customers. It’s priced at $30 per user/month​ (and requires the customer already have a Microsoft 365 E3, E5 or Business Standard/Premium license). As of early 2024, Copilot is rolling out to enterprise customers at this pricing. (There is no consumer or educational availability at the moment outside of trials – it’s focused on enterprise value.) Microsoft 365 Copilot – 一個內建於 Microsoft Office 365 套件（Word、Excel、PowerPoint、Outlook、Teams）中的 AI 助手。Copilot 使用 OpenAI 的 GPT-4 來協助用戶在這些應用程式中提高生產力。例如，在 Word 中可以根據提示或資料撰寫文件，在 Excel 中可以分析資料並建立公式或摘要（「告訴我這個電子表格的洞察」），在 PowerPoint 中可以根據大綱產生簡報，在 Outlook 中可以撰寫或回覆郵件。在 Teams 中，它還能即時提供會議摘要。功能：深度整合用戶的檔案與情境，可以從日曆、郵件和文件中提取相關資訊，以客製化其回應。價格：Microsoft 365 Copilot 是針對商業 Microsoft 365 用戶的附加功能，每位用戶每月收費 30 美元（且用戶必須已擁有 Microsoft 365 E3、E5 或 Business Standard/Premium 授權）。截至 2024 年初，Copilot 正以這個價格向企業用戶推廣。（目前尚無消費者或教育用途的版本，僅限於試用，專注於企業價值。）

    Google Workspace Duet AI – Google’s answer to AI in productivity apps (branded as Duet AI , formerly part of Google Labs). It provides AI assistance across Google Docs, Sheets, Slides, Gmail, and Meet. Examples: “Help me write” in Gmail or Docs will draft emails and documents from a prompt, automatic meeting summaries in Google Meet, generate images for slides in Google Slides, and even ChatGPT-like Q&A in Google Chat. Features: In Docs and Gmail, users can refine the AI output by tone (“make it more formal”), in Sheets, you can get formula help or generate sample data. In Google Meet, Duet can even capture notes and action items live. Pricing: Google is offering Duet AI to business customers at $30 per user/month (similar to Microsoft’s pricing. This is an add-on to Google Workspace Enterprise plans. Google did allow free trials in 2023, but going forward it’s a paid subscription for businesses. Some AI features (like basic Smart Compose or grammar suggestions) remain free for all users in Gmail/Docs, but the advanced generative capabilities are part of this paid package. (Duet AI is still in rollout; as of late 2024, Google renamed parts of it as Gemini AI  for Workspace, with the same pricing.) Google Workspace Duet AI – Google 的 AI 解決方案，應用於生產力應用程式（品牌為 Duet AI，原為 Google Labs 的一部分）。它提供跨 Google Docs、Sheets、Slides、Gmail 和 Meet 的 AI 協助。範例：在 Gmail 或 Docs 中的「幫我寫」功能，可根據提示草擬郵件和文件；Google Meet 中自動產生會議摘要；Google Slides 中生成幻燈片圖片，甚至 Google Chat 中有類似 ChatGPT 的 Q&A 功能。功能：在 Docs 和 Gmail 中，用戶可以透過語氣調整（如「讓它更正式」）來修飾 AI 產生的內容；在 Sheets 中，可獲得公式協助或產生範例資料。在 Google Meet 中，Duet 還能即時記錄筆記和行動項目。價格：Google 向企業用戶提供 Duet AI，費用為每位用戶每月 30 美元（與 Microsoft 的價格類似）。此為 Google Workspace 企業方案的附加服務。Google 在 2023 年曾允許免費試用，但從此後企業用戶需訂閱付費。部分 AI 功能（如基本的 Smart Compose 或語法建議）在 Gmail/Docs 中仍對所有用戶免費，但進階的生成性功能則包含在這個付費方案中。 (目前 Duet AI 還在逐步推出中；截至 2024 年年底，Google 已將其部分功能重新命名為 Gemini AI for Workspace，價格相同。)

    Zoom AI Companion – A productivity AI for Zoom users. Zoom’s AI Companion (formerly Zoom IQ) can generate meeting summaries, next-step suggestions, and even chat message drafts. During Zoom Meetings, it can record and transcribe the discussion live, highlight key points, and afterwards produce an auto-generated summary for those who missed the meeting. In Zoom Team Chat, it can write reply suggestions. Pricing: Notably, Zoom has decided to include AI Companion for free with paid Zoom accounts​. Any user with a licensed (paid) Zoom plan can use these AI features at no extra cost​. (Free Zoom users do not have AI Companion access as of now.) This move (announced in 2023) means organizations already paying for Zoom can leverage AI summaries without an additional fee, yielding potential cost savings (Zoom is positioning it against separate transcript services). The AI Companion is enabled by default on paid plans (like Pro, Business, Enterprise), making it very accessible to many businesses and educators. Zoom AI Companion – 針對 Zoom 使用者打造的生產力 AI。Zoom 的 AI Companion（原為 Zoom IQ）可以產生會議摘要、下一步建議，甚至聊天訊息草稿。在 Zoom 會議中，它可以即時錄音並轉譯討論內容，強調重點，並在會後自動產生摘要，供錯過會議的人參考。在 Zoom 小組聊天中，它也能提供回覆建議。價格：值得注意的是，Zoom 已決定將 AI Companion 免費包含在付費 Zoom 帳號中。任何擁有授權（付費）Zoom 方案的用戶都可以免費使用這些 AI 功能。（目前免費 Zoom 使用者無法使用 AI Companion。）此舉（於 2023 年宣布）意味著已經付費使用 Zoom 的組織，可以無需額外費用就使用 AI 摘要功能，這可能帶來潛在的成本節省（Zoom 是將其定位為對抗獨立轉譯服務的方案）。AI Companion 在付費方案（如 Pro、Business、Enterprise）中預設啟用，使其對許多企業和教育工作者來說非常容易取得。)

    Slack GPT – (Emerging; included for context.)  Slack (the team messaging app) is developing built-in AI features (called Slack GPT) that will be able to summarize channels, draft messages, and retrieve information. This is experimental and likely will leverage Salesforce’s Einstein GPT (Salesforce owns Slack). Pricing and full capabilities are TBD, but it’s expected to be included for Slack users (possibly some features for free, with advanced functionality for paying customers). Keep an eye on Slack’s updates for when it fully launches. Slack GPT – (新興; 供參考用途。) Slack（團隊即時通訊應用程式）正在開發內建的 AI 功能（稱為 Slack GPT），這些功能將能總結頻道、草擬訊息以及檢索資訊。這項功能目前為實驗性質，預期會使用 Salesforce 的 Einstein GPT（Salesforce 擁有 Slack）。價格與完整功能尚未確定，但預期會包含在 Slack 用戶的使用範圍內（可能部分功能免費，進階功能則需付費用戶）。請留意 Slack 的更新，以掌握其正式發佈的時機。

    Data Analysis and Business Intelligence AI Tools 資料分析與商業智慧 AI 工具

    Tableau – A leading Business Intelligence (BI) and data visualization tool, now augmented with AI-powered analytics. Tableau allows users to create interactive dashboards and reports from various data sources. Tableau – 領先的商業智慧（BI）與資料視覺化工具，現已加入 AI 驅動的分析功能。Tableau 讓用戶能從多種資料來源建立互動式儀表板與報告。

    Recent AI features in Tableau include “Ask Data”, which lets you ask questions in natural language (e.g., “Show sales by region for 2023”) and it generates a chart for you, and “Explain Data”, which uses AI to provide possible explanations for outliers or trends in a visualization​. Tableau is also introducing Tableau GPT and Pulse, which proactively surface insights in plain language​. Tableau 近期推出的 AI 功能包括「Ask Data」，讓您可以用自然語言提問（例如：「顯示 2023 年各區域的銷售情況」），並自动生成圖表，以及「Explain Data」，利用 AI 提供視覺化資料中異常值或趨勢的可能解釋。Tableau 也正在推出 Tableau GPT 與 Pulse，這些功能將以平易近人的語言主動呈現洞察。

    Pricing: Tableau is sold per user: Creator license at $70–$75/user/month (billed annually) gives full authoring power​. Explorer (for users who explore and edit existing content) is ~$42/user/month, and Viewer (view-only) is ~$15/user/month. There is a free public version ( Tableau Public ) for non-confidential data, and a limited free trial. Enterprise deployments may use Tableau Server or Cloud with those same per-user costs. (AI features like Ask Data are included in these licenses – no extra fee, they are part of the platform.) 定價：Tableau 是按使用者計費的。Creator 授權為每位使用者每月 $70–$75（年度計費），提供完整的創作功能。Explorer（適用於瀏覽與編輯現有內容的使用者）為每位使用者每月約 $42，而 Viewer（僅觀看）為每位使用者每月約 $15。對於非機密資料，有免費公開版本（Tableau Public）以及有限的免費試用版。企業部署可使用 Tableau Server 或 Cloud，其費用與上述每位使用者的費用相同。（AI 功能如 Ask Data 已包含在這些授權中，無需額外費用，它們是平台的一部分。）

    Microsoft Power BI – Microsoft’s BI and data visualization platform, which heavily integrates AI features. Power BI enables the creation of dashboards and reports with interactive charts, and it can use AI to help analyze data. For example, the Power BI Q&A feature allows users to ask questions in plain English – “What was the total sales last month by product?” – and it will generate the answer with a chart or number​. Microsoft Power BI – 微軟的 BI 與資料視覺化平台，並大量整合 AI 功能。Power BI 可以使用互動式圖表來建立儀表板和報告，並能利用 AI 來協助分析資料。例如，Power BI 的 Q&A 功能允許使用者以自然英文提問 – 「上個月各產品的總銷售額是多少？」– 並會以圖表或數字產生答案。

    Power BI also includes “Key Influencers” visual (an AI visual that analyzes which factors most impact a given metric) and “Decomposition Tree” (which uses AI to drill down into data hierarchies by importance). Power BI 還包含「Key Influencers」視覺元件（一種 AI 視覺元件，用來分析哪些因素最影響特定指標）以及「Decomposition Tree」（利用 AI 按重要性深入分析資料層級）。

    Pricing: Power BI has a desktop app that’s free for creating reports. To share and use in cloud: Power BI Pro is $9.99 per user/month (increasing to $13.99 in 2025), which allows report sharing and basic AI visuals. 定價：Power BI 有一個免費的桌面應用程式，可用於建立報告。要分享並在雲端使用：Power BI Pro 每用戶每月 $9.99（2025 年將提高至 $13.99），允許報告分享與基本的 AI 視覺化功能。

    Power BI Premium exists for heavier workloads – either $20 per user/month (soon $24) for Premium Per User​, or capacity-based (starting ~$4,995/month for the dedicated cloud capacity, used by large enterprises). Power BI Premium 用於處理較重的負載 – Premium Per User 每用戶每月 $20（將很快提高至 $24），或以容量為基礎（專用雲端容量起價約為每月 $4,995，主要用於大型企業）。

    The AI features (Q&A, AI visuals) are available in Pro, while Premium adds AutoML for dataset predictions and other advanced AI. Microsoft often includes Power BI Pro in certain Office 365 enterprise bundles, making it widely available in businesses. It’s a cost-effective option with robust AI for analysis. AI 功能（問答、AI 視覺化）在 Pro 中可用，而 Premium 則加入 AutoML 用於資料集預測及其他進階 AI 功能。微軟經常將 Power BI Pro 包含在某些 Office 365 企業套件中，使其在企業中廣泛可用。這是一個具備強大 AI 分析功能且成本效益高的選擇。

    DataRobot – An enterprise AI platform for Automated Machine Learning (AutoML) and predictive analytics. DataRobot enables data scientists and analysts to feed in data and automatically train/evaluate dozens of machine learning models (classification, regression, time-series) to find the best performer. DataRobot – 一個企業用的 AI 平台，用於自動化機器學習（AutoML）和預測分析。DataRobot 讓資料科學家和分析師可以輸入資料，並自動訓練與評估數十種機器學習模型（分類、回歸、時間序列），以找出表現最佳的模型。

    It provides explainability on models (why a prediction was made) and tools to deploy models into production. DataRobot is used in industries to build AI models for things like demand forecasting, customer churn prediction, or academic research, without hand-coding each model. 它提供模型的可解釋性（為何會做出預測）以及將模型部署至生產環境的工具。DataRobot 被用於各產業中建立 AI 模型，用於需求預測、客戶流失預測或學術研究，而無需手動編碼每個模型。

    Features: automation of feature engineering, model training and tuning; a leaderboard of model performance; built-in guardrails to avoid overfitting; and MLOps tools to monitor models. 功能：自動化特徵工程、模型訓練與調參；模型表現的排行榜；內建的防護措施以避免過度擬合；以及 MLOps 工具來監測模型。

    Pricing: DataRobot is an enterprise software – flexible pricing customized to the client’s needs​. They don’t publicize fixed prices; instead it often depends on number of users, number of models or servers, and level of support. 價格：DataRobot 是企業軟體，提供根據客戶需求量身打造的彈性價格方案。他們不會公開固定價格；價格通常取決於用戶數量、模型或伺服器數量，以及支援等級。

    Users report that DataRobot is a significant investment (six-figure annual subscriptions are common for mid-size deployments, and it’s considered premium priced  in the AutoML market)​. 使用者表示 DataRobot 是一項重大投資（中型部署常見的年費訂閱費為六位數，且在 AutoML 市場中被視為高價產品）​。

    DataRobot does sometimes offer trial licenses or academic programs, and has cloud-hosted and on-prem options. In summary, expect to engage with DataRobot sales for a quote; it’s positioned for enterprises willing to invest substantially in AI development. DataRobot 有時會提供試用授權或學術計畫，並有雲端主機與本地部署的選項。總結來說，預期需要與 DataRobot 的銷售團隊接洽以取得報價；它主要針對願意在 AI 開發上大幅投資的企業。

    H2O.ai (Driverless AI) – H2O.ai provides both an open-source machine learning library (H2O-3) and a commercial AutoML platform called Driverless AI. H2O.ai (Driverless AI) – H2O.ai 提供一個開源的機器學習函數庫 (H2O-3) 以及一個商業的 AutoML 平台，稱為 Driverless AI。

    Driverless AI is an AutoML tool that automatically tries various algorithms (including advanced techniques) and feature engineering to create the best predictive model, with a focus on interpretability and performance. It includes built-in machine learning interpretability (LIME, Shapley values) to explain models. Driverless AI 是一個 AutoML 工具，會自動嘗試各種演算法（包括高階技術）與特徵工程，以建立最佳的預測模型，並重視模型的可解釋性與表現。它內建機器學習的可解釋性功能（如 LIME、Shapley 值）來說明模型。

    Features: time series modeling support, automatic visualization insights, the ability to include your own custom algorithms or scripts, and training pipelines that can be exported (e.g., as Java or Python code) for deployment. 功能：支援時間序列模型、自動視覺化洞察、可加入自定義的演算法或腳本，以及可以導出訓練流程（例如，作為 Java 或 Python 程式碼）以進行部署。

    Pricing: H2O’s core library is free and open-source. Driverless AI (enterprise) is a paid product. H2O offers an enterprise AI Cloud starting around $50,000 per unit, sold in multi-unit packages (minimum 4 units = ~$200,000) for a full deployment​. 定價：H2O 的核心庫是免費且開源的。Driverless AI（企業版）則為付費產品。H2O 提供企業 AI 雲端服務，每單位約需 5 萬美元起，以多單位包裝銷售（最低 4 單位 = 約 20 萬美元）以實現完整部署。

    This would support a team with robust infrastructure. However, smaller installations or H2O Driverless AI licenses can be obtained on the cloud marketplaces (AWS, Azure) on shorter term – e.g., some listings show an Annual edition for $80k/year for 5 users on AWS​. 這適用於擁有強大基礎設施的團隊。然而，較小規模的安裝或 H2O Driverless AI 授權可以透過雲端市場（如 AWS、Azure）以較短的合約期取得 – 例如，某些清單顯示 AWS 上每年 8 萬美元的年度版，可供 5 名使用者使用。

    They also have trial versions. In short, H2O.ai follows a typical enterprise pricing model: open-source for basic use, expensive enterprise licenses for the full featured AutoML with support (targeting large organizations). 他們也提供試用版本。總而言之，H2O.ai 跟隨典型的企業定價模式：基本用途為開源免費，而完整的 AutoML 功能搭配支援則需要昂貴的企業授權（主要針對大型組織）。

    Dataiku – A collaborative data science platform that allows data analysts, scientists, and engineers to work together on data preparation, analytics, and machine learning. Dataiku – 一個協作的數據科學平台，讓數據分析師、科學家和工程師能夠共同進行數據準備、分析和機器學習。

    Dataiku provides a graphical interface for building data pipelines (extract, clean, join data) and then training models, plus a coding interface for those who want to write Python/R. Dataiku 提供圖形化介面用於建立資料流程（抽取、清理、合併資料），並進行模型訓練，同時也提供程式編寫介面，供想用 Python/R 進行撰寫的使用者使用。

    It’s popular in enterprises to operationalize AI projects across teams. 在企業中，跨團隊實作 AI 專案是很常見的。

    Features: a visual recipe interface (no-code for common data transformations), AutoML for creating models without coding, ability to bring your own code and libraries, and deployment/monitoring tools. It also has plug-ins for deep learning, NLP, etc. 功能：包含視覺化食譜介面（無需程式碼即可進行常見的資料轉換）、AutoML 用於無需程式碼即可建立模型、可自帶自己的程式碼與函式庫，以及部署與監控工具。它還支援深度學習、NLP 等插件。

    Pricing : Dataiku has a few editions. There is a Free edition (user-local installation) that allows up to 3 users and limited data volumes – great for learning or small academic projects​. 價格：Dataiku 有幾個版本。其中有一個免費版（用戶端安裝），允許最多 3 名使用者，且資料量有限 – 非常適合學習或小型學術專案。

    Beyond that, Dataiku Lite/Team (sometimes called Discover ) might start around $70k–$80k per year for ~5 users on limited infrastructure​. Full Dataiku Enterprise can cost in the hundreds of thousands per year for larger user counts and high-performance connectors. 除了上述之外，Dataiku Lite/Team（有時也稱為 Discover）在有限基礎設施下，約五名用戶的年度費用可能在 7 萬到 8 萬美元左右。完整的 Dataiku Enterprise 則可能因用戶數量較多及高性能連接器而每年耗費數十萬美元。

    (For example, 290 users at one company was cited at $1M/year​.) Dataiku also offers Dataiku Cloud, a SaaS offering with more accessible plans – they mention “plans designed for smaller organizations”  on their site​. （例如，有家公司提到 290 名用戶的年度費用為 100 萬美元。）Dataiku 還提供 Dataiku Cloud，這是一項 SaaS 服務，擁有更易接觸的方案 – 他們網站上提到了「為小型組織設計的方案」。

    But generally, expect Dataiku to be a significant investment beyond the free tier. Many mid/large enterprises find the collaboration and governance features worth the cost, whereas small teams or academics might stick to the free version. 但總體而言，預期 Dataiku 在免費層級之外會是一筆相當大的投資。許多中型或大型企業認為其協作與治理功能值得這筆開支，而小型團隊或學術研究者則可能持續使用免費版本。

    RapidMiner & KNIME (Open-Source Analytics) – Honorable mentions: RapidMiner & KNIME（開放原始碼分析） – 值得一提的選項：  

    These platforms provide GUI-based data science. KNIME Analytics Platform is free and open-source, allowing drag-and-drop creation of data workflows for analysis and modeling​. It’s often used in academia due to zero cost and supports extensions for text, images, etc. (KNIME’s enterprise server for collaboration is paid, but using the tool locally is completely free even in commercial settings.) 這些平台提供圖形化使用者介面（GUI）的資料科學功能。KNIME Analytics Platform 是免費且開源的，允許使用者透過拖曳方式建立資料工作流程，用於分析與建模。它常被用於學術領域，因為完全免費，也支援文字、影像等擴充功能。（KNIME 的企業伺服器用於協作是付費的，但即使在商業環境中，使用該工具本地端仍是完全免費的。）

    RapidMiner (now partly open core) similarly offers an easy UI for data prep and AutoML, with community editions free and paid studio licenses for enterprise. Both are good for those who want to do data analysis without coding, albeit with possibly less flexibility than coding frameworks. RapidMiner（現已部分開放核心）同樣提供一個簡單的使用者介面，用於資料預處理與 AutoML。社群版為免費，企業版則提供付費的 Studio 授權。這兩種工具都適合那些不想寫程式就進行資料分析的使用者，不過可能在靈活性上不如寫程式的框架。

    Finance and FinTech AI Tools 財務與金融科技 AI 工具

    Bloomberg Terminal (w/ BloombergGPT) – The Bloomberg Terminal is a staple data system in finance, and Bloomberg has integrated AI to help users surface information faster. Bloomberg Terminal（搭配 BloombergGPT）– Bloomberg Terminal 是財務領域中不可或缺的資料系統，而 Bloomberg 已整合 AI 技術，協助使用者更快地取得資訊。

    BloombergGPT is a domain-specific large language model trained on financial data that Bloomberg launched in 2023. It is used to power advanced search and NLP on the Terminal​. BloombergGPT 是彭博於 2023 年推出的專門用於金融領域的大型語言模型，其訓練資料來自金融數據。它被用來強化終端機上的高階搜尋與自然語言處理功能。  

    Use cases: a trader or analyst can ask the system questions in plain English – “What’s the sentiment on company X in the news today?” – and BloombergGPT can perform sentiment analysis across news and social data, or answer questions using the Terminal’s vast data​. It also can assist in tasks like generating a summary of a financial report or extracting key metrics from filings. 應用場景：交易員或分析師可以以自然英文向系統提問，例如「今天新聞中對公司 X 的觀感如何？」，BloombergGPT 可以跨新聞與社交數據進行情緒分析，或利用終端機龐大的數據來回答問題。它也能協助完成如財務報告摘要生成或從 filings 中提取關鍵指標等任務。

    Pricing: The Bloomberg Terminal itself is a premium product, costing about $25,000–$30,000 per user per year​. 價格：彭博終端機本身是高階產品，每位用戶每年約需支付 25,000 至 30,000 美元。

    (As of 2025, around $2,500 per month.) The AI capabilities are included for Terminal subscribers; BloombergGPT is not sold standalone, but rather enhances the Terminal’s value. So essentially, the cost to use Bloomberg’s AI is the cost of the Terminal subscription. （截至 2025 年，約為每月 2,500 美元。）AI 功能已包含在終端機訂閱服務中；BloombergGPT 不是單獨銷售，而是用來提升終端機的價值。因此，使用彭博 AI 的費用，其實就是終端機訂閱的費用。

    This makes it mostly accessible to financial institutions, trading firms, and research analysts who already invest in Bloomberg. 這使得該服務主要對已經投資 Bloomberg 的金融機構、交易公司及研究分析師開放。

    Zest AI – An AI-driven credit underwriting platform used in the financial services industry. Zest AI – 一個用於金融服務產業的 AI 驅動信用評估平台。

    Zest AI builds custom machine learning models for lenders (banks, credit unions) to improve credit decisions – helping identify good borrowers that might be missed by traditional credit scores and ensuring decisions are fair and compliant. Zest AI 為貸款機構（銀行、信用合作社）建立客製化的機器學習模型，以提升信用決策的準確性 – 帮助識別傳統信用分數可能忽略的優質借款人，並確保決策的公平與合規。

    Features: Zest’s platform takes in historical loan performance data and relevant variables, then produces an AI model that predicts risk; it also provides explainability for each decision (to satisfy regulations and adverse action notices) and tools for bias testing to maintain fairness​. 功能：Zest 的平台會接收歷史貸款表現資料及相關變數，然後產生預測風險的 AI 模型；同時也提供每個決策的說明（以符合監管要求及反對行動通知），並提供偏誤測試工具以維持公平性。

    Financial institutions use Zest to increase approval rates and reduce defaults simultaneously. Pricing: Zest AI is an enterprise SaaS and provides tailored pricing based on the size of the lender and portfolio. They do not publish prices; interested organizations must contact sales​. 金融機構使用 Zest 來同時提高核准率並降低違約率。價格：Zest AI 是企業 SaaS 服務，根據貸款人規模及貸款組合提供客製化價格。他們不會公開價格；感興趣的機構必須聯繫銷售部門。

    For context, customers have indicated it’s a significant but worthy expense (since it potentially saves or makes millions in loan interest). There is no self-serve or free version – it’s a partnership (often with onboarding fees, annual license fees, etc.). 就背景而言，客戶表示這是一筆重要的但值得的開支（因為它潛在地可節省或創造數百萬的貸款利息）。目前沒有自助服務或免費版本 – 它是一種合作關係（通常會有上手費用、年度授權費用等）。

    Feedzai – A leading AI platform for fraud detection and financial crime prevention. Banks, payment processors, and merchants use Feedzai to monitor transactions in real time and score them for fraud risk. Feedzai’s AI models analyze various data (transaction details, device info, user behavior) to identify suspicious patterns (credit card fraud, money laundering, account takeovers) and can block or flag high-risk events. Feedzai – 一個在詐欺偵測與金融犯罪預防方面領先的 AI 平台。銀行、支付處理商與商家使用 Feedzai 來即時監測交易並評估其詐欺風險。Feedzai 的 AI 模型會分析各種資料（交易細節、設備資訊、用戶行為）以識別可疑模式（信用卡詐欺、洗錢、帳戶接管）並可阻止或標記高風險事件。

    Features: Feedzai provides a 360° view of customers by aggregating data and uses machine learning for anomaly detection. It also offers case management for investigators to review flagged incidents​. The platform can handle massive volumes – e.g., scoring every card swipe or online purchase within milliseconds. 功能：Feedzai 提供 360° 的客戶視圖，透過整合資料並使用機器學習進行異常偵測。它也提供案例管理功能，讓調查人員可以檢視標記的事件。此平台可處理大量資料 – 例如，在毫秒內為每張卡片刷卡或線上交易進行評分。

    Clients: major institutions like Citibank, Standard Chartered, and others use Feedzai globally​ . 客戶：像 Citibank、Standard Chartered 等主要機構在全球使用 Feedzai。

    Pricing: Feedzai is delivered as enterprise software (or cloud service) with pricing typically based on the scale of operations (number of transactions analyzed, etc.). 價格：Feedzai 以企業軟體（或雲端服務）形式提供，價格通常根據運作規模（分析的交易數量等）而定。

    It’s usually a custom annual subscription or license. As a reference, it’s known to be a multi-million dollar investment for large banks (given it protects billions in transactions). 通常是自訂的年度訂閱或授權。作為參考，對大型銀行而言，這被認為是數百萬美元的投資（因為它保護了數十億美元的交易）。

    No public price tiers are available; Feedzai’s value proposition is reducing fraud loss and compliance fines, which justifies its cost to large customers. 沒有公開的價格層級；Feedzai 的價值主張在於降低詐欺損失與合規罰款，這對大型客戶而言足以證明其成本的合理性。

    AlphaSense – An AI-powered search engine for market intelligence and research. AlphaSense is used by financial analysts, researchers, and corporate strategy teams to search through a vast library of business information: investor call transcripts, SEC filings, company presentations, news articles, and equity research. AlphaSense – 一個以人工智慧為核心的市場情報與研究搜尋引擎。AlphaSense 被財務分析師、研究人員及企業策略團隊使用，用以搜尋龐大的商業資訊庫：投資者電話會議紀錄、證券交易委員會（SEC）文件、公司簡報、新聞文章以及股票研究報告。

    Its AI semantics go beyond keyword matching – you can search a concept or question, and AlphaSense will retrieve relevant snippets across millions of documents, using NLP to understand context. Features: fast search with filters for company, industry, etc.; smart synopses that highlight why a result is relevant; and an AI-driven Insight Generator . AlphaSense also recently integrated generative AI to allow Q&A style interaction (e.g., “Summarize the outlook of company X based on recent earnings calls”). 其人工智慧語義功能超越關鍵字匹配 – 你可以搜尋一個概念或問題，AlphaSense 會透過數百萬份文件中擷取相關片段，並利用自然語言處理（NLP）來理解上下文。功能包括：快速搜尋並可依公司、產業等條件篩選；智慧摘要功能強調結果相關性；以及由人工智慧驅動的洞察生成器。AlphaSense 最近也整合了生成式人工智慧，以允許問答式互動（例如：「根據公司 X 最近的財務電話會議，總結其未來展望」）。

    Pricing: AlphaSense is sold via annual subscription, usually to firms (it’s not a cheap individual tool). It offers enterprise packages and per-seat options​. 價格：AlphaSense 透過年度訂閱方式銷售，通常針對機構（它不是一個便宜的個人工具）。它提供企業版套件以及每座位選項。

    The exact price varies – reports suggest it can be $20k+ per year for a team license, or a smaller team could opt for a seat-based pricing maybe in the mid-four figures per seat. The vendor emphasizes flexibility (likely meaning they will quote based on content access and user count)​. 精確的價格會有所不同 – 報導指出，團隊授權的價格每年可能高達 2 萬美元以上，較小的團隊則可能選擇以座位為單位的計費方式，每座位約在四千美元左右。供應商強調靈活性（很可能是指他們會根據內容存取量和用戶數量來報價）​。

    It does not have a free tier; however, free trials or pilot programs might be available. Generally used by investment firms, consultancies, universities, and corporate intel departments that can invest in premium research tools. 它沒有免費版本；不過，免費試用或試點計畫可能還是可以取得的。通常被投資機構、顧問公司、大學以及企業智囊部門使用，這些機構可以負擔高階研究工具的費用。

    Numerai (Numerai Signals) – (Example of experimental finance AI).  Numerai is a hedge fund that crowdsources models from data scientists through weekly tournaments. Participants build AI models on encrypted market data and submit predictions, staking cryptocurrency on their performance. Numerai（Numerai Signals） – （實驗性金融 AI 的範例）。Numerai 是一個避險基金，透過每週的競賽向資料科學家徵集模型。參與者在加密的市場資料上建立 AI 模型，並提交預測，以加密貨幣作為他們表現的賭注。

    While not a tool that a business “buys,” it exemplifies AI in finance – an open platform where hundreds of models vote on trades. 雖然這不是企業「購買」的工具，但它體現了金融領域的 AI 應用 – 一個開放平台，讓數百個模型共同投票決定交易。

    In a related vein, Kensho (owned by S&P Global) offers AI analytics like event-driven insights for finance, and Bloomberg’s Alpaca and Kavout are AI-driven platforms for stock selection. These are more specialized or in-house rather than widely available off-the-shelf products. 在相關領域，Kensho（由 S&P Global 擁有）提供如事件驅動洞察等 AI 分析工具用於金融業，而 Bloomberg 的 Alpaca 和 Kavout 則是用於股票選擇的 AI 驅動平台。這些工具較為專業化或為內部開發，而非廣泛使用的現成產品。

    (Overall, finance adoption of AI is often internal or bespoke – large banks build proprietary AI for algorithmic trading, risk management, etc. 總體而言，金融業對 AI 的採用多為內部或客製化的方式——大型銀行會建立專屬的 AI 系統用於算法交易、風險管理等。

    The tools listed above, like Zest and Feedzai, show how some niche processes have their own AI vendors. 上述提到的工具，如 Zest 和 Feedzai，顯示出某些特定流程已有專屬的 AI 供應商。

    For broad use, many finance professionals leverage general tools like Python ML libraries or platforms like DataRobot mentioned earlier to create custom models for their specific financial datasets.) 若要廣泛應用，許多金融專業人士會利用一般的工具，如 Python 的機器學習庫，或前述提到的 DataRobot 等平台，來為其特定的金融數據集建立自定義模型。

    Healthcare and Medical AI Tools 醫療與醫療 AI 工具

    PathAI – A leading AI platform in digital pathology. PathAI develops AI algorithms that assist pathologists in analyzing histopathology slides (e.g., cancer biopsies). For instance, PathAI’s models can detect and quantify cancerous cells, grading tumor samples for severity, or identify biomarkers (like certain protein expressions) with high consistency​ . This helps improve accuracy and efficiency in diagnosis. PathAI often partners with hospitals (such as the Cleveland Clinic and others)​ and pharmaceutical companies (for AI analysis in clinical trials). PathAI – 在數位病理科領域的領導 AI 平台。PathAI 開發 AI 演算法，協助病理科醫師分析組織切片（例如癌症活檢）。例如，PathAI 的模型可以偵測並量化癌細胞，評估腫瘤樣本的嚴重程度，或以高一致性識別生物標記（如某些蛋白質表現）​。這有助於提升診斷的準確性與效率。PathAI 常與醫院（如克利夫蘭克利夫蘭診療中心等）​及藥廠公司合作（用於臨床試驗中的 AI 分析）。

    Usage: integrated into pathology workflows via digital slide scanners – pathologists see AI-marked regions of interest and quantifications (e.g., % of tumor area). 使用方式：透過數位切片掃描儀整合至病理科工作流程 – 病理科醫師可看到 AI 標註的興趣區域與量化結果（例如腫瘤面積百分比）。

    Regulation: These tools often require FDA approvals; PathAI is involved in studies and some of its solutions are investigational or used in research settings currently. 規範：這些工具通常需要 FDA 核准；PathAI 參與相關研究，目前部分解決方案仍處於研究或臨床試驗階段。

    Pricing: PathAI works on a B2B model – it sells its platform (like AISight ) to health systems and labs, likely as a software license or service contract. Not public, but presumably priced in line with high-end medical imaging software. (For reference, adoption involves significant investment in digital pathology infrastructure. With Quest Diagnostics acquiring PathAI’s diagnostics arm​, we may see its AI reach many labs commercially.) 價格：PathAI 以 B2B 模式運作 – 它將其平台（例如 AISight）銷售給醫療系統與實驗室，可能是以軟體授權或服務合約的方式。目前尚未公開，但預計價格與高端醫療影像軟體相當。(作為參考，採用此系統需要在數位病理基礎設施上進行大量投資。隨著 Quest Diagnostics 收購 PathAI 的診斷部門，我們可能看到其 AI 技術在商業上廣泛應用於許多實驗室。)

    Viz.ai – An AI-powered diagnostic and care coordination platform that is widely deployed for certain acute conditions like stroke. Viz.ai’s first FDA-cleared tool was for stroke detection on CT scans: it uses AI to identify a large vessel occlusion (LVO) stroke from a CT angiogram and immediately alert the neurologist on call (via a mobile app). This can save precious minutes in stroke treatment. Viz.ai – 一個以 AI 為核心的診斷與照護協調平台，廣泛應用於某些急性病症，例如中風。Viz.ai 首個獲得 FDA 認證的工具是用於 CT 扫描的中風偵測：它利用 AI 來識別 CT 血管造影中的大血管阻塞（LVO）中風，並立即透過行動應用程式通知當值神經學家。這可以為中風治療節省寶貴的時間。

    Features: beyond stroke, Viz.ai has expanded modules for pulmonary embolism detection, aortic aneurysms, intracerebral hemorrhage, and even EKG analysis for hypertrophic cardiomyopathy​ . 功能：除了中風之外，Viz.ai 還擴展了其他模組，包括肺栓塞偵測、主動脈瘤、腦內出血，甚至還有用於肥厚型心肌病的 EKG 分析。

    It also functions as a communication platform – once it detects an issue, it shares images and notifies the specialist team to coordinate rapid care. 它同時也作為一個溝通平台 – 一旦偵測到問題，就會分享影像並通知專科團隊以協調快速照護。

    Adoption: Viz.ai is in over 1,500 hospitals in the US and has over 45,000 medical providers using it​. 採用：Viz.ai 現已於美國超過 1,500 家醫院使用，並有超過 45,000 名醫療人員在使用​。

    It’s even becoming a standard of care in stroke triage. Pricing: Viz.ai is offered as an enterprise software subscription to hospitals. 它甚至逐漸成為腦中風篩查的標準照護方式。價格：Viz.ai 是以企業軟體訂閱方式提供給醫院。

    The pricing is not public, but typically it could be a fixed annual fee per hospital or imaging volume. 價格並未公開，但通常可能是每家醫院或影像量收取固定年度費用。

    Given it addresses critical care, hospitals justify the cost with improved patient outcomes and reimbursement for faster treatment. 由於其處理關鍵照護的特性，醫院會以改善病患結果及更快治療的賠償為由，來合理化其成本。

    For context, similar triage AI solutions often range from low to mid five figures USD per year per institution (depending on modules). Viz.ai being a market leader with multiple modules might be on the higher end (some hospitals have noted costs but under NDA). 在這個背景下，類似的篩選 AI 解決方案每年每機構的費用通常介於低至中等五位數美元之間（視模組而定）。Viz.ai 作為市場領導者，擁有許多模組，可能在較高範疇（有些醫院已提及費用，但屬於保密協議）。

    Aidoc – Another prominent radiology AI company offering a suite of FDA-cleared algorithms. Aidoc’s AI runs in the background of a radiology PACS system and flags critical findings: for example, intracranial hemorrhage on head CT, pulmonary embolism on chest CT, spine fractures, or intra-abdominal free air. Aidoc – 另一家著名的放射科 AI 公司，提供一系列 FDA 認證的演算法。Aidoc 的 AI 在放射科 PACS 系統後台運行，並標記關鍵發現：例如頭部 CT 的顱內出血、胸部 CT 的肺栓塞、脊椎骨折或腹腔內自由氣體。

    It then alerts radiologists of the possible finding so they can prioritize that study. Features: Aidoc provides an “always-on” AI second reader for over a dozen conditions, and an unified worklist that highlights AI-positive cases. 它隨後會提醒放射科醫生可能的發現，使其能優先處理該檢查。功能：Aidoc 提供一個「持續運作」的 AI 第二讀者，用於超過十種病症，並提供統一的工作清單，突出 AI 判斷為陽性的案例。

    It also recently introduced an AI care coordination layer (similar to Viz) to activate care teams. Usage: Many hospitals and teleradiology groups use Aidoc to improve ER imaging turnaround. Pricing: Aidoc sells to imaging providers with pricing often based on the number of scans analyzed or per institution license. 它最近也推出了一層 AI 照護協調功能（類似於 Viz），以啟動照護團隊。使用方式：許多醫院和遠距放射科群組使用 Aidoc 來提升急診影像的處理速度。價格：Aidoc 向影像服務提供者銷售，價格通常根據分析的掃描數量或每機構授權來計算。

    Again, exact prices are not public; pricing can be modular (buy each algorithm or as a bundle). A mid-size hospital might pay somewhere in the range of $ hundreds of thousands per year for a full suite covering multiple modalities – but ROI comes from optimized radiologist workflow and potential medical legal benefits of catching misses. Aidoc often showcases improved metrics (like reduced report turnaround for critical cases by >30%). 再次說明，精確的價格並未公開；定價可以模組化（買單一算法或整套方案）。一個中型醫院每年可能支付數十萬美元來購買一套涵蓋多種模態的完整系統，但投資回報來自於優化放射科醫師的工作流程，以及在發現遺漏病例時可能帶來的醫療法律上的好處。Aidoc 通常會展示改善的指標（例如在關鍵病例中減少報告處理時間超過 30%）。

    IBM watsonx (Watson) for Healthcare – IBM’s Watson gained fame for Jeopardy, and IBM attempted to apply Watson AI to healthcare (notably in oncology). IBM watsonx（Watson）於醫療領域的應用 – IBM 的 Watson 因在《危險邊界》（Jeopardy）節目中的表現而聞名，IBM 隨後嘗試將 Watson AI 應用於醫療領域（特別是在腫瘤學方面）。

    Watson for Oncology  was a system developed with Memorial Sloan Kettering to recommend cancer treatments, but it faced challenges and was ultimately not widely adopted (IBM sold off Watson Health assets in 2022). Watson for Oncology 是與梅約克洛斯癌症中心合作開發的系統，用來推薦癌症治療方案，但該系統面臨許多挑戰，最終並未廣泛採用（IBM 於 2022 年出售了 Watson Health 的資產）。

    Today, IBM’s healthcare AI efforts are refocused under Watsonx, with a shift to providing toolkits (NLP for clinical notes, decision support modules) rather than a monolithic doctor-facing product. 目前，IBM 的醫療 AI 計畫已重新聚焦於 Watsonx，轉向提供工具組（如用於臨床筆記的自然語言處理、決策支援模組），而非單一面向醫生的產品。

    Features : IBM offers clinical NLP to extract information from medical records (e.g., identify diagnoses, medications), and has Watson Assistant for patient engagement (chatbots answering health questions or guiding insurance members). 功能：IBM 提供臨床自然語言處理（NLP）以從醫療記錄中提取資訊（例如，識別診斷、藥物），並擁有 Watson Assistant 用於患者參與（聊天機器人回答健康問題或引導保險會員）。  

    Pricing: IBM’s healthcare solutions are enterprise offerings – e.g., a hospital might license an NLP service to integrate into their EMR, or a insurance company might pay per member for a Watson-based engagement solution. 價格：IBM 的醫療保健解決方案是企業級產品 – 例如，醫院可能會取得 NLP 服務的授權，整合至其電子病歷系統，或保險公司可能會根據每位會員收費，以使用基於 Watson 的參與解決方案。

    Since IBM is now more B2B infrastructure here, the pricing is custom and typically part of larger IT contracts. (For context, IBM Watson Assistant for healthcare might start at a base fee plus usage, similar to Watson Assistant pricing in general – e.g., $1400/month for a decent user volume deployment – but healthcare configurations can be significantly more once integration and compliance are factored in.) 由於 IBM 現在在這方面更偏向 B2B 基礎設施，價格通常是客製化且通常為較大的 IT 合約的一部分。（為提供背景資訊，IBM Watson Assistant 在醫療保健領域的價格可能從基本費用加使用量開始，與一般 Watson Assistant 的價格模式相似 – 例如，一個相當用戶量的部署可能每月 $1400 – 但一旦考慮整合與合規性，醫療保健配置的費用可能大幅增加。）

    Ada Health – A widely-used symptom checker app powered by AI, aimed at consumers. Ada is like a digital triage tool: it asks the user a dynamic series of medical questions (using an expert system + AI) about their symptoms and health history, and then provides a potential list of conditions (“possible causes”) and recommended next steps (e.g., self-care advice or see a doctor). Ada Health – 一個廣為使用的 AI 驅動症狀檢查 APP，主要針對消費者。Ada 就像是數位的篩檢工具：它會透過專家系統加上 AI，向使用者提問一系列動態的醫療問題，並根據症狀與健康史提供可能的疾病清單（「可能病因」）以及建議的下一步行動（例如自癒建議或就醫）。

    Use cases: patient-facing app (13+ million users worldwide, with tens of millions of symptom assessments run)​; also licensed to health systems and insurers to guide patients to the right care. 應用場景：面向患者的 APP（全球擁有 1300 萬以上用戶，進行數千萬次症狀評估）；同時也授權給醫療系統與保險公司，用以引導患者尋求適當的照護。

    Features: conversational interface, large medical knowledge base, personalized questions based on earlier answers. Ada also supports multiple languages. 功能：對話式介面、龐大的醫療知識庫、根據先前回答提供個人化問題。Ada 也支援多種語言。

    Pricing : For individual users, Ada is free on mobile (it monetizes via partnerships and licensing). For enterprise clients (clinics, insurers), Ada offers an API or white-label integration, usually under a SaaS contract. 價格：對於個人用戶，Ada 在行動裝置上是免費的（透過合作夥伴關係與授權來實現營收）。對於企業客戶（如診所、保險公司），Ada 提供 API 或白標整合方案，通常是在 SaaS 合約下進行。

    Pricing enterprise-wise can vary (possibly per user assessed or flat fees for population usage). Ada’s value to partners is reducing unnecessary doctor visits and directing people appropriately, which has cost-saving implications. 企業的定價方式可能不同（可能是根據用戶評估或針對人口使用收取固定費用）。Ada 對合作夥伴的價值在於減少不必要的就醫次數，並適當引導民眾，這有節省成本的潛在效益。

    Babylon Health – (Note: Babylon Health had offered a similar AI symptom triage chatbot and even virtual GP services in the UK and other countries. It faced business challenges recently. Its AI symptom checker was free for users via app, while healthcare providers or governments paid for telehealth services around it. Babylon’s case shows both the promise and pitfalls of AI in primary care triage.) Babylon Health – （注意：Babylon Health 曾在英國及其他國家提供類似的 AI 症狀篩查聊天機器人，甚至虛擬家庭醫生服務。近期它面臨了一些商業挑戰。其 AI 症狀檢查器對用戶而言是透過應用程式免費提供的，而醫療保健提供者或政府則需為其周圍的遠距醫療服務付款。Babylon 的案例顯示出 AI 在門診篩查中的潛力與潛在風險。）

    Corti – An AI tool used in emergency dispatch centers. Corti’s algorithm listens to emergency calls (with caller consent) and in real-time tries to detect signs of critical events (like cardiac arrest) from the caller’s descriptions and background sounds. It can prompt the dispatcher if certain keywords or patterns indicate, say, the patient isn’t breathing, so they can quickly start CPR instructions. This is a niche but life-saving AI use. Pricing would be a service contract with EMS agencies (custom). Corti – 用於緊急派遣中心的 AI 工具。Corti 的演算法會聆聽緊急電話（需經通話者同意），並在實時中嘗試從通話者的描述及背景聲音中偵測關鍵事件的跡象（例如心臟停搏）。如果某些關鍵字或模式顯示患者已無呼吸，它會提示派遣員，讓他們迅速開始心肺復甦術的指導。這是一種專業但能挽救生命的 AI 應用。價格將以與 EMS 機構的服務合約形式訂定（客製化）。

    AlphaFold (DeepMind) – An AI system that solved the protein folding problem, predicting 3D structures of proteins. While not a business “tool” in a traditional sense, AlphaFold’s open database of millions of protein structures  is widely used in academic research and drug discovery​ . AlphaFold (DeepMind) – 一個解決蛋白質摺疊問題的 AI 系統，可預測蛋白質的 3D 結構。雖然不算是傳統意義上的商業「工具」，但 AlphaFold 提供的數百萬個蛋白質結構的開放資料庫，廣泛應用於學術研究與藥物開發​ 。

    DeepMind released AlphaFold predictions for the scientific community for free. Companies like DeepMind (now Google DeepMind) and others are continuing such experimental AI which impacts academia significantly. DeepMind 為科學界免費釋出 AlphaFold 的預測結果。像 DeepMind（現為 Google DeepMind）這樣的公司以及其他機構，持續進行這種影響學術界極大的實驗性 AI 研究。

    (Overall in healthcare, many AI tools are either highly specialized (cleared for one diagnostic task) or broad but underutilized. （整體而言，在醫療領域，許多 AI 工具或是高度專門化（僅核准單一診斷任務），或是範圍廣泛但使用率不高。

    Adoption is growing in medical imaging (radiology, pathology) and administrative tasks (coding, transcribing). 在醫療影像（放射科、病理科）及行政任務（編碼、轉錄）方面的採用率正在增加。

    The cost of entry (and regulatory approval) means widely available tools are often through healthcare providers rather than directly to end-users, except symptom checkers or wellness apps.) 進入門檻（以及監管核准）意味著廣泛可用的工具通常透過醫療提供者而非直接提供給終端使用者，除非是症狀檢查器或健康應用程式。

    Coding and Software Development AI Tools 程式設計與軟體開發 AI 工具

    GitHub Copilot – An “AI pair programmer” integrated into code editors like VS Code, Visual Studio, JetBrains IDEs, etc. Copilot uses OpenAI Codex (GPT-based model trained on code) to suggest the next lines or blocks of code as you type. GitHub Copilot – 一種「AI 對程式設計師」工具，整合於 VS Code、Visual Studio、JetBrains IDE 等程式編輯器中。Copilot 使用 OpenAI Codex（基於 GPT 的模型，透過大量程式碼訓練而成）來建議您輸入時的下一行或一段程式碼。

    It can complete whole functions given a comment description or even generate unit tests, helping developers code faster and with fewer context switches. 它可以根據註解描述完成整個函數，甚至產生單元測試，協助開發者更快地進行程式設計，並減少情境切換的次數。

    Features: inline code completion, multi-line suggestions, and Copilot can also be invoked explicitly to get suggestions for docstrings or complex logic. It supports dozens of programming languages. 功能：支援內嵌程式碼補全、多行建議，並可明確呼叫 Copilot 以取得文件字串或複雜邏輯的建議。它支援數十種程式語言。

    Pricing: Copilot is a paid service at $10 per month (or $100/year) for individuals​. It’s free for certain users: verified students, teachers, and popular open-source project maintainers get Copilot for free​ .  There’s also Copilot for Business at $19 per user/month (which includes extra admin controls and secure model versions)​. Copilot’s popularity has made it a common tool in many developers’ workflow since its general availability in mid-2022​ . 價格：Copilot 是一個付費服務，個人用戶每月 $10（或每年 $100）。某些用戶可免費使用：經驗證的學生、教師以及知名開源專案維護者可免費取得 Copilot。此外，還有 Copilot for Business，每位使用者每月 $19（包含額外的管理控制和安全模型版本）。自 2022 年中間推出以來，Copilot 的人氣使其成為許多開發者工作流程中常見的工具。

    Tabnine – An AI code completion tool that predates Copilot and offers code snippet suggestions. Tabnine runs either on cloud or local (depending on plan) and predicts code based on context, also completing whole lines or function signatures. It supports multiple languages and IDEs. Tabnine can be configured to use open-source model suggestions or even fine-tuned on your own code repository for more relevant completions (in higher tiers). Pricing: Tabnine has a Free plan (community model, basic completions)​ . The Pro plan is $12 per user/month (annual billing), which unlocks advanced AI models (including their own large models) and more customization​. An Enterprise plan (~$39/user/month) allows self-hosting and private model training on your codebase for maximum security and accuracy​. (Tabnine’s free tier is good for individual hobbyists; companies often choose Enterprise for on-prem deployment so source code doesn’t leave their environment.) Tabnine – 一個在 Copilot 之前就存在的 AI 程式碼補全工具，提供程式碼片段建議。Tabnine 可以在雲端或本地端運行（視訂閱方案而定），並根據上下文預測程式碼，也能完成整行或函數簽名。它支援多種語言和 IDE。Tabnine 可以設定使用開源模型建議，甚至在更高階的方案中，可以針對自己的程式碼倉庫進行微調，以獲得更相關的補全建議。價格：Tabnine 提供免費方案（社群模型，基本補全功能）。Pro 方案為每位用戶每月 12 美元（年度計費），解鎖進階 AI 模型（包括其自有大型模型）和更多自訂功能。企業方案（約每位用戶每月 39 美元）允許自建伺服器並在自己的程式碼庫上進行私人模型訓練，以達到最高安全性和準確性。（Tabnine 的免費方案適合個人愛好者使用；公司通常會選擇企業方案進行內部部署，以確保程式碼不離開其環境。）

    Amazon CodeWhisperer – AWS’s AI coding assistant, similar to Copilot, focused on helping developers who use AWS services. CodeWhisperer integrates with IDEs (like AWS Cloud9, VS Code, JetBrains) and suggests code, especially snippets that call AWS APIs correctly (which is a strong suit given it’s trained on Amazon’s own documentation and codebase). Features: generation of code blocks for tasks (for example, writing a Python function to upload to S3), security scanning for vulnerabilities, and reference tracking (it can identify if a suggestion is very similar to open-source code and warn about licenses). Pricing: CodeWhisperer has a notable Free tier for individual developers with unlimited code completions​. For professional use with admin controls, CodeWhisperer Professional costs $19 per user/month. The Professional tier adds enterprise features like organizational policy management and higher limits on the built-in security scans (500 scans/month vs 50 on free) ​ . This pricing (free vs $19) makes it attractive – Amazon positioned it as free for individual use even compared to Copilot’s paid model​. (Note: The name was recently changed to Amazon Q Developer, but commonly still referred to as CodeWhisperer.) Amazon CodeWhisperer – AWS 的 AI 程式助手，類似於 Copilot，專注於協助使用 AWS 服務的開發者。CodeWhisperer 可與 IDE（例如 AWS Cloud9、VS Code、JetBrains）整合，並建議程式碼，特別是正確呼叫 AWS API 的片段（這一點尤其強大，因為它是基於 Amazon 自己的文件與程式碼庫進行訓練的）。功能包括為任務生成程式碼區塊（例如撰寫一個 Python 函數上傳至 S3）、安全性掃描以偵測漏洞，以及參考追蹤（它可以辨識建議的程式碼是否與開源程式碼非常相似，並提醒相關授權問題）。價格：CodeWhisperer 對於個人開發者有顯著的免費層，提供無限的程式碼補全功能。對於需要管理員控制的專業用途，CodeWhisperer Professional 價格為每位使用者每月 $19。Professional 層次還增加了企業功能，例如組織策略管理，以及內建安全性掃描更高的上限（每月 500 次掃描，而免費層為 50 次）。此價格策略（免費 vs $19）使其更具吸引力 – Amazon 將其定位為即使與 Copilot 的付費模式相比，個人使用也完全免費。 (注意：這個名稱最近已更名為 Amazon Q Developer，但仍然常被稱為 CodeWhisperer。)

    Replit Ghostwriter – An AI coding assistant integrated into Replit, the online IDE. Ghostwriter can autocomplete code, explain code, and even chat with the programmer to help fix bugs or implement features. It’s designed for a seamless experience in a browser-based development environment. Features: a chat sidebar in Replit where you can ask for help (“Why is this function not returning the right value?”), generate code from a prompt, or get explanations of code. Ghostwriter supports a range of languages that Replit supports. Pricing: Ghostwriter is part of Replit’s paid plans. It used to be offered for $10/month as a separate add-on ​ , but now Replit has bundled it into their Pro plan at $20/month (which includes Ghostwriter along with other benefits like private Repls and more computing power)​. Students and educators can apply for free Ghostwriter access via Replit’s education initiatives. For enterprises or teams, Replit offers a $40/user/month plan (with advanced features like Ghostwriter chat over your team’s codebase)​ . Replit Ghostwriter – 結合於 Replit 的 AI 程式助手，Replit 是一個線上整合開發環境。Ghostwriter 可以自動完成程式碼、解釋程式碼，甚至與程式設計師對話以協助修復錯誤或實現功能。它專為瀏覽器端的開發環境設計，提供順暢的使用體驗。功能：Replit 的側邊欄聊天功能，你可以提出問題（「為何這個函數沒有回傳正確的值？」），根據提示生成程式碼，或取得程式碼的解釋。Ghostwriter 支援 Replit 所支援的多種語言。價格：Ghostwriter 是 Replit 支付計畫的一部分。它曾經作為獨立的附加功能以每月 10 美元的價格提供，但現在已整合至 Replit 的 Pro 計划中，每月 20 美元（包含 Ghostwriter 及其他功能，如私人 Repls 和更多計算資源）。學生和教育工作者可以透過 Replit 的教育計畫申請免費使用 Ghostwriter。對於企業或團隊，Replit 提供每月 40 美元的用戶計畫（包含進階功能，如在團隊程式碼庫上使用 Ghostwriter 聊天）。

    Codeium – A free AI code completion tool that has emerged as an open alternative to Copilot. Codeium offers IDE extensions that provide suggestions and autocompletion similarly to Copilot/Tabnine. It supports many languages and frameworks and has a chat-like assistant as well. Features: unlimited usage for individuals, context-aware suggestions, and ability to self-host for enterprise. Codeium – 一個免費的 AI 程式碼補全工具，作為 Copilot 的開放源碼替代方案而興起。Codeium 提供 IDE 擴充功能，提供類似 Copilot/Tabnine 的建議與自動補全功能。它支援許多語言與框架，並具備類似聊天的助理功能。功能：個人用戶可無限使用，情境感知建議，以及企業自建伺服器的選項。

    Pricing: Free for individual developers, forever​. Codeium monetizes via an enterprise offering – organizations can get Codeium for Teams/Enterprise with self-host options, starting around $20–$39 per user/month depending on needs​ . 價格：對個人開發者免費，永遠免費。Codeium 透過企業方案來獲取收入 – 組織可以取得 Codeium for Teams/Enterprise 自建伺服器選項，每位用戶每月約需$20–$39，視需求而定。

    The enterprise version provides private model deployment (so your code doesn’t go to Codeium’s cloud) and admin controls. 企業版提供私有模型部署（因此您的程式碼不會上傳至 Codeium 的雲端），並有管理員控制功能。

    The generous free tier has made Codeium popular among students, open-source contributors, and budget-conscious devs as it provides a Copilot-like experience at no cost. 這項慷慨的免費方案讓 Codeium 在學生、開放源碼貢獻者以及預算有限的開發者之間非常受歡迎，因為它能免費提供類似 Copilot 的使用體驗。

    Sourcegraph Cody – An AI coding assistant by Sourcegraph, focused on using your repository’s code and docs to answer questions. Sourcegraph Cody – 一個由 Sourcegraph 提供的 AI 程式碼助手，專注於利用您的倉庫中的程式碼和文件來回答問題。

    Cody can index your entire codebase and then answer questions like “How does the user authentication workflow work in our app?” It uses a local context window of your code to provide highly relevant answers or even generate new code in the style of your codebase. Cody 可以索引您的整個程式碼庫，並回答類似「我們的應用程式中用戶認證流程是如何運作的？」這樣的问题。它會使用您程式碼的本地情境視窗，提供高度相關的答案，甚至能根據您的程式碼風格生成新的程式碼。

    Features: integrates with Sourcegraph (a code search engine) – you can highlight code and ask Cody to explain or refactor it. It can also generate unit tests and help with large-scale codebase navigation. 功能：與 Sourcegraph（一個程式碼搜尋引擎）整合 – 您可以標註程式碼並請 Cody 解釋或重構它。它也能生成單元測試，並協助在大型程式碼庫中導航。

    Pricing:  Sourcegraph offers Cody for free on public open-source repos and for small personal repositories. For companies, it’s part of Sourcegraph Enterprise – pricing in the range of $39 per user/month for the Teams plan, with higher tiers for bigger organizations​. (It’s relatively new; Sourcegraph likely negotiates custom enterprise deals, and they offer a self-hosted version for privacy.) 價格：Sourcegraph 在公開的開源倉庫和小型個人倉庫上提供 Cody 無償使用。對於企業來說，它是 Sourcegraph Enterprise 的一部分 – 團隊方案的價格約為每位用戶每月 39 美元，較大的組織則有更高階的方案​。 （這項服務相對較新；Sourcegraph 可能會與企業進行客製化協議，並提供自建版本以確保隱私。）

    JetBrains AI Assistant – (In preview) JetBrains (maker of IntelliJ, PyCharm, etc.) is integrating an AI assistant into its IDEs, offering code completions and chat. It currently works with models like OpenAI or local LLMs as backends. Once fully released, it will likely be included for users of JetBrains IDEs (potentially requiring a JetBrains subscription and OpenAI API key for now – no extra fee from JetBrains side yet). This will give another option especially for developers already using those IDEs. JetBrains AI Assistant – (預覽中) JetBrains（IntelliJ、PyCharm 等的製造商）正在將 AI 助手整合至其 IDE 中，提供程式碼補全與聊天功能。目前它與 OpenAI 或本地 LLMs 等模型合作作為後端。一旦正式發佈，它將很可能包含在 JetBrains IDE 的用戶端（目前可能需要 JetBrains 訂閱和 OpenAI API 金鑰 – 但 JetBrains 還未收取額外費用）。這將為已經使用這些 IDE 的開發者提供另一個選擇。

    (Overall, AI coding assistants have quickly become ubiquitous. Many developers might use one of the above daily. Open-source and self-hostable options are notable for academia or companies with strict IP policies. The pricing trend is around $10/month for individual devs and ~$20-$40 for enterprise per seat with added control. We can expect integrated offerings (like from Microsoft, Amazon, JetBrains) to continue as well.) （總體而言，AI 程式碼助手已經迅速成為常見工具。許多開發者可能每天都會使用上述其中一種。開源與自建的選項在學術界或有嚴格版權政策的公司中尤其值得注意。價格趨勢大致為每位個人開發者每月 10 美元，企業版則為每位座位 20 到 40 美元，並提供更多控制權。我們可以預期像 Microsoft、Amazon、JetBrains 這樣的整合方案會持續出現。）

    1. Customer Service and Chatbot AI Platforms
    2. 客戶服務與聊天機器人 AI 平台

    IBM Watson Assistant – A platform for building AI chatbots and virtual agents that can handle customer inquiries. Watson Assistant provides a dialog designer, integrates IBM’s Natural Language Understanding, and can connect to various channels (web chat, phone via Twilio, messaging apps). It allows enterprises to create bots for customer support or internal helpdesk that understand user intents and provide answers or perform tasks. Features: pre-built content for common domains, the ability to search FAQs or knowledge bases for answers, and support for voice (with Watson’s speech-to-text and text-to-speech). Watson Assistant is known for its enterprise focus – data privacy, integration with IBM systems, and multilingual support. Pricing: Watson Assistant has a Lite plan (free)  for getting started (limited monthly active users). Paid plans typically start at $140/month for an instance that includes 1,000 monthly active users, with overage charges per 100 additional users​ .  

    The pricing model can be by MAUs (monthly active users) plus resource utilization. IBM offers custom pricing for large enterprise deployments (with voice IVR, multiple chatbots, high volume).  

    The Plus plan example is $140 for 1,000 users, then $14 per additional 100 users​. IBM also has an option where it charges by API calls (or “messages”) if not using the MAU model. In summary, small deployments might cost a few hundred per month, whereas large ones can run into thousands or more monthly, depending on user engagement. Plus 方案的範例是 1,000 位使用者$140，之後每增加 100 位使用者則為$14。IBM 也有另一種計費方式，若不使用 MAU 模型，則按 API 呼叫（或「訊息」）計費。總結來說，小型部署每月可能僅需數百美元，而大型部署則可能高達數千甚至更多，這取決於使用者的參與度。

    Google Dialogflow – Google’s conversational AI platform for building chatbots, available in two versions: Dialogflow ES (standard) and Dialogflow CX (advanced for complex flows). Dialogflow uses Google’s NLU to parse user intents and entities, and designers can create dialogue routes accordingly. It integrates easily with Google Cloud telephony (for voice bots) and messaging channels. Google Dialogflow – Google 的對話式 AI 平台，用於建立聊天機器人，提供兩種版本：Dialogflow ES（標準版）和 Dialogflow CX（用於複雜流程的高階版）。Dialogflow 使用 Google 的自然語言理解（NLU）來解析使用者的意圖與實體，設計師可以根據此建立對話流程。它很容易與 Google Cloud 的電話服務（用於語音機器人）和通訊頻道整合。

    Features: rich entity extraction, context management for follow-up intents, and a straightforward web UI to build bots. It also supports fulfillment via webhooks (for dynamic responses or actions). Pricing: Dialogflow ES has a free usage quota (e.g., the first 180 texts/minute sessions per month are free) and then charges per request roughly $0.002 per text interaction and $0.0065 per 15 seconds for voice​. In practice, that’s ~$0.75 per 1,000 text messages​. Dialogflow CX (for large-scale bots) uses a session model: about $20 per 100 sessions for text (each session can include multiple turns)​. For instance, 1,000 CX conversations would cost ~$200. There’s also a trial credit ($600) for new customers. Small bots might incur just a few dollars a month; big enterprise bots with millions of messages would scale accordingly. Because it’s pay-as-you-go with Google Cloud, it’s accessible to all sizes (no monthly minimum). 功能：豐富的實體抽取、支援追蹤意圖的上下文管理，以及直觀的網頁介面來建立聊天機器人。它也支援透過 Webhook 實現 fulfillment（用於動態回應或操作）。價格：Dialogflow ES 有免費使用配額（例如每月前 180 則文字/分鐘的會話為免費），之後按每次請求計費，約為每則文字互動 $0.002，每 15 秒語音 $0.0065。實際上，這相當於每 1,000 則文字訊息約 $0.75。Dialogflow CX（用於大型機器人）採用會話模型：文字每 100 個會話約 $20（每個會話可包含多個對話回合）。例如，1,000 個 CX 對話會話約需 $200。新客戶還有試用信用額度（$600）。小型機器人可能每月僅需幾美元；而處理數百萬則訊息的企業級機器人則會根據使用量進行擴展。因為採用 Google Cloud 的按使用量計費模式，所以無論規模大小皆可使用（無月費最低限制）。

    Amazon Lex – AWS’s service for building conversational interfaces and powering chatbots (text or voice) using the same technology that Alexa uses for ASR and NLU. Lex allows developers to define intents, sample utterances, and slot types (entities). It can integrate with AWS Lambda to fulfill actions (e.g., update an order status). Features: automatic speech recognition if using voice, multi-turn conversations with slot elicitation (the bot asks for missing info), and deep integration with other AWS services. Pricing: Amazon Lex is pay-per-request. Text-based conversations cost about $0.00075 per request (message)​. For voice (speech in/out), it’s $0.004 per voice request (or $0.0065 per 15 sec for streaming audio)​. Amazon Lex – AWS 的服務，用於建立對話介面並透過 Alexa 所使用的 ASR 和 NLU 技術來驅動聊天機器人（文字或語音）。Lex 讓開發者可以定義意圖（intents）、示例語句（sample utterances）以及槽位類型（entities）。它可與 AWS Lambda 結合以執行動作（例如更新訂單狀態）。功能包括：若使用語音則具備自動語音辨識、多輪對話與槽位引導（bot 會詢問缺少的資訊），以及與其他 AWS 服務深度整合。價格：Amazon Lex 是按請求計費。文字對話每請求（訊息）約為 $0.00075。語音（語音輸入輸出）每語音請求為 $0.004（或每 15 秒 $0.0065 的串流音訊費用）。

    AWS also offers a free tier for Lex: 10,000 text requests and 5,000 voice requests per month for the first year​. This means for 100,000 messages, you’d pay roughly $75. The cost can be quite economical, and like other AWS services, it scales with usage. Amazon positions Lex for enterprise as well, often alongside Amazon Connect (their cloud call center) to provide AI IVR. There are no subscription fees; it is purely usage-based. AWS 還提供 Lex 的免費層：第一年每月 10,000 個文字請求和 5,000 個語音請求。這意味著對於 100,000 個訊息，費用約為 $75。成本相當經濟，且如同其他 AWS 服務一樣，會隨著使用量而擴展。Amazon 將 Lex 定位為企業用途，常與 Amazon Connect（他們的雲端客服中心）搭配使用，以提供 AI 電話自動應答系統（IVR）。沒有訂閱費用；它完全是根據使用量計費。

    Ada – (Ada Support) Ada – (Ada 支援)

    Many large companies use an AI customer service automation platform to deflect and handle customer inquiries. Companies can design conversational flows in Ada’s builder, and Ada’s AI helps map varied customer inputs to the correct flows or answers. Ada emphasizes quick integration with existing CRMs and systems (Salesforce, Zendesk, etc.), allowing the bot to pull account info or perform actions so that the bot can entirely handle many routine requests (resetting a password, checking order status). 許多大型企業使用 AI 客服自動化平台來轉移並處理客戶查詢。企業可以使用 Ada 的建構工具設計對話流程，而 Ada 的 AI 會協助將多樣化的客戶輸入對應到正確的流程或回應。Ada 強調快速整合現有的 CRM 與系統（如 Salesforce、Zendesk 等），讓機器人可以提取帳號資訊或執行操作，以完全處理許多常見的請求（如重置密碼、查詢訂單狀態）。

    Features: Generative AI responses—Ada recently introduced an AI “Brain” that can use large language models to answer questions from knowledge base articles (with oversight)​, multi-channel deployment (web widget, WhatsApp, etc.), and a fallback to human agents when needed. 功能：生成式 AI 回應—Ada 最近推出了一個 AI「大腦」，可以使用大型語言模型從知識庫文章中回答問題（並有監督機制），多渠道部署（網頁小工具、WhatsApp 等），以及在需要時轉接人類客服人員。

    Clients: Ada is used by brands like Meta, Shopify, AirAsia, and many fintech and e-commerce companies. 客戶：Ada 被 Meta、Shopify、AirAsia 等品牌以及許多金融科技和電商公司所使用。

    Pricing: Ada doesn’t publicize pricing; it’s an enterprise SaaS with custom quotes. It typically charges based on the number of resolved conversations or monthly active users, with base platform fees. 價格：Ada 沒有公開價格資訊；它是一個企業用的 SaaS 服務，提供客製化報價。通常根據解決的對話數量或每月活躍用戶數來計費，並收取基本平台費用。

    As a benchmark, for a mid-sized enterprise, Ada might charge a base fee plus usage in the $5k—$15k per month range, scaling up with volume. 作為一個參考標準，對於中型企業而言，Ada 可能會收取基本費用加上每月 $5,000 至 $15,000 的使用費用，費用會根據使用量增加而調整。

    (However, they likely tailor pricing to be ROI-positive compared to hiring more support staff – often promoting that Ada’s AI agent can handle the equivalent of many support FTEs at a fraction of cost​.) They offer a demo and usually some pilot program. （不過，他們通常會根據成本效益來調整價格，使其相比於聘請更多支援人員更具投資回報率 – 他們常宣傳 Ada 的 AI 代理可以以極低的成本處理相當於許多支援全職員工的工作。）他們提供試用版，通常也會提供一些試點計畫。

    Intercom Fin / Custom GPT bots – Many customer support software providers recently integrated GPT. For example, Intercom (a popular support chat platform) launched an add-on called “Fin” – an AI bot that can answer from your existing Intercom knowledge base. Intercom Fin / 自訂 GPT 代理 – 很多客戶支援軟體供應商最近都整合了 GPT。例如，Intercom（一個廣受歡迎的支援聊天平台）推出了一個名為「Fin」的附加功能 – 一個 AI 代理，可以從您現有的 Intercom 知識庫中回答問題。

    It essentially uses OpenAI under the hood but wrapped with Intercom’s context and falls back to humans if they are unsure. Intercom’s AI is offered to customers of Intercom’s higher-tier plans, likely as an add-on with its pricing (currently in early access; pricing rumored to be usage-based or a fixed uplift). 它基本上使用的是 OpenAI 的技術，但透過 Intercom 的情境進行包裝，如果 AI 不確定答案，就會轉交給人類處理。Intercom 的 AI 服務僅提供給使用其高階方案的客戶，可能作為附加功能來收費（目前處於早期試用階段；價格預計可能是基於使用量或固定費用增加）。

    Similarly, Zendesk has introduced the Zendesk Answer Bot with Advanced AI, which uses a similar approach to better handle tickets with LLMs. These are typically charged as premium features on top of normal licensing (for instance, Zendesk’s AI add-on might be an extra $50-$70/agent/month for advanced bots, as some industry chatter suggests). 同樣地，Zendesk 也推出了搭配先進 AI 的 Zendesk Answer Bot，其採用類似的方法，以更好地處理票券。這些功能通常是基於標準授權之上作為高階功能收費（例如，Zendesk 的 AI 增強套件可能為每個代理每月額外 $50-$70，如某些產業消息所提及的）。

    Rasa (Open Source) – An open-source framework for building custom conversational AI chatbots. Rasa is a developer-oriented toolkit: you define intents, entities, and dialogue rules (or use machine learning policies to learn dialogue). It gives complete control and can be self-hosted, so data stays on-prem. Features: Rasa NLU (natural language understanding) for intent classification & entity extraction, Rasa Core for dialogue management, and lots of customization – you can inject custom Python code at any step. Rasa（開放原始碼）– 一個用來建立自訂對話式 AI 聊天機器人的開放原始碼框架。Rasa 是一個以開發者為導向的工具組：你可以定義意圖、實體與對話規則（或使用機器學習政策來學習對話）。它提供完整的控制權，且可以自架設，因此資料會留在本地端。功能包括：Rasa NLU（自然語言理解）用於意圖分類與實體抽取、Rasa Core 用於對話管理，以及許多自訂選項 – 你可以在任何階段插入自訂的 Python 程式碼。

    Pricing: Rasa Open Source is free to use (Apache 2.0 license). They offer Rasa Pro/Enterprise, which includes a managed platform, enterprise-grade analytics, and support. Rasa Enterprise is a paid subscription typically negotiated per production instance or chatbot. (They introduced a “free Rasa Pro” license for one bot with up to 1k monthly conversations to entice companies; beyond that, it’s paid)​ . 價格：Rasa Open Source 可免費使用（Apache 2.0 授權條款）。他們提供 Rasa Pro/Enterprise，包含管理平台、企業等級的分析功能與支援。Rasa Enterprise 是一種付費訂閱方案，通常依生產實例或聊天機器人的數量進行協議。他們曾推出「免費 Rasa Pro」授權，適用於最多一個機器人且每月最多 1,000 次對話的情況，以吸引企業使用；超過此範圍則需付費。

    Large enterprises can expect to pay for support and scaling – but Rasa doesn’t disclose rates publicly. The key point is that if you have in-house developers, Rasa lets you build without licensing costs, and then you only pay if you need official support or their enterprise dashboard. Many academic projects use Rasa for free, and some companies run Rasa OS on their infrastructure to avoid SaaS fees. 大型企業預期會為支援與擴展功能付費，但 Rasa 並未公開收費標準。重點在於，如果你有內部開發人員，Rasa 讓你以無授權費用的方式進行開發，僅在需要官方支援或企業版看板時才需付費。許多學術專案都免費使用 Rasa，一些公司則在其基礎設施上運行 Rasa OS 以避免 SaaS 費用。

    1. Education and Research AI Tools
    2. 教育與研究 AI 工具

    Elicit (by Ought) – Elicit（由 Ought 開發）–

    An AI research assistant tool that helps scholars and learners find relevant papers and answer research questions. Elicit allows a user to input a natural language question (especially ones that would be answered by academic literature, e.g., “What are the effects of X on Y according to recent studies?”). It then uses language models and a paper corpus (papers from Semantic Scholar) to find relevant publications and summarize the findings​. It also can brainstorm research ideas or summarize a given paper. 一個協助學者與學習者尋找相關論文並回答研究問題的 AI 研究助理工具。Elicit 讓使用者輸入自然語言問題（尤其是那些會由學術文獻回答的問題，例如：「根據最近的研究，X 對 Y 有什麼影響？」）。它隨後會使用語言模型與論文資料庫（來自 Semantic Scholar 的論文）來尋找相關出版品並總結研究結果。它也能協助產生研究點子或總結指定的論文。

    Features: literature review assistance – it surfaces not just keyword matches. Still, it looks at the context (thanks to the LLM), semantic paper search, and a tool to compare snippets from multiple papers answering the question. Pricing: Elicit is free to use. It’s a nonprofit research lab (Ought) project, and they’ve kept it open for the community. (No login required; heavy users can create a free account to save searches.) Since grants fund it, academics benefit from full access at no cost. This makes it a popular experimental tool for quick paper discovery in graduate student circles. 功能：文獻回顧協助 – 它不僅僅顯示關鍵字匹配，同時也會考量上下文（感謝 LLM 的協助），語義化的論文搜尋，以及一個比較多篇論文片段回答同一問題的工具。價格：Elicit 可以免費使用。它是非營利研究實驗室（Ought）的專案，他們將其對社群開放。 （無需登入；重度使用者可以建立免費帳號來儲存搜尋。）由於有研究經費支撐，學術界可以免費使用完整功能。這使得它成為研究生圈中快速發現論文的熱門實驗工具。

    Semantic Scholar & AI-powered features – Semantic Scholar is an academic search engine (by Allen Institute for AI) indexes over 200 million papers. 語義學者與 AI 功能 – Semantic Scholar 是一個學術搜尋引擎（由 Allen Institute for AI 開發），索引超過 2 億篇論文。

    It has incorporated AI in features like TL;DR summaries (automatically generated one-sentence summaries of papers) and a semantic recommendation system (“similar papers”). It also recently introduced Semantic Reader with Co-Pilot, an experimental PDF reader that shows an AI sidebar answering questions about the paper, explaining acronyms, and summarizing sections – effectively using an LLM fine-tuned scientific text. 它已整合 AI 功能，例如 TL;DR 摘要（自動生成的論文單句摘要）和語義推薦系統（「相似論文」）。它最近也推出了 Semantic Reader 搭配 Co-Pilot，這是一個實驗性的 PDF 閱讀器，會顯示一個 AI 側邊欄來回答與論文相關的問題、解釋縮寫以及摘要各個段落 – 有效地使用了一個針對科學文獻微調的 LLM。

    Pricing: Semantic Scholar is free for researchers. The AI features (summaries, etc.) are provided openly. The Semantic Reader AI Co-Pilot is in beta (available for select papers via a waitlist or partnership, e.g., with arXiv papers). Academic institutions might collaborate with AI2 for broader access, but currently, it’s all free as it’s a research initiative. 價格：Semantic Scholar 對研究者是免費的。AI 功能（如摘要等）皆公開提供。Semantic Reader 的 AI Co-Pilot 目前處於測試階段（僅部分論文透過等候名單或合作夥伴提供，例如與 arXiv 合作的論文）。學術機構可能與 AI2 合作以獲得更廣泛的使用權，但目前所有功能皆為免費，因為這是一個研究計畫。

    Scite – An AI tool for analyzing scientific citation statements. Scite lets you see how a paper is cited by later papers – specifically; it uses NLP to classify whether citations are supporting, contrasting, or just mentioning the referenced work. This helps researchers quickly gauge the reputation or impact  of a paper’s findings (e.g. if multiple later studies contradict  the original claim). Scite – 一個用來分析科學文獻引用語句的 AI 工具。Scite 讓你看到一篇論文是如何被後續文獻引用的，特別是它使用自然語言處理技術來分類引用是支持、反駁，或是僅提及被引用的文獻。這有助於研究者快速評估一篇論文的聲譽或影響力（例如，若有多篇後續研究反駁原始論點）。

    Scite also has an AI assistant feature. You can ask a question, and it will try to answer with evidence from papers (providing cited sources). Pricing: Scite has a free tier (limited number of citation look-ups per month). Scite 還有 AI 助理的功能。你可以提出問題，它會嘗試以文獻中的證據來回答（並提供被引用的來源）。價格：Scite 提供免費層（每月有限制的引用查詢次數）。

    Premium personal plans are about $10/month for academics (for unlimited site reports and AI assistant queries). Institutional licenses are available for libraries (so students and faculty can all use them under the university IP range). The value for paying is in terms of extensive usage and API access. 高階個人方案約為每月 10 美元，適用於學術研究者（提供無限制的網站報告與 AI 助理查詢）。機構授權則可供圖書館使用（讓學生與教職員工都能在大學 IP 範圍內使用）。付費的價值在於廣泛使用與 API 存取。

    For casual use, the free account (up to ~5 AI answers and 100 citation searches per month) might suffice, but active researchers may subscribe to get unlimited access. 對於輕度使用，免費帳號（每月最多約 5 次 AI 回答與 100 次引用查詢）可能已經足夠，但積極從事研究的學者可能選擇訂閱以獲得無限制的使用權。

    ChatGPT (for educational use) – Many students and researchers use general LLMs like ChatGPT or Claude to assist with studying or research in various ways: explaining complex concepts, generating quiz questions, translating passages, proofreading, brainstorming thesis ideas, summarizing articles, etc. ChatGPT（用於教育用途）– 很多學生與研究者會使用像 ChatGPT 或 Claude 這類一般的 LLMs 來協助學習或研究，方式包括解釋複雜概念、產生測驗題目、翻譯段落、校對、腦力激盪論文點子、總結文章等。

    While we discussed ChatGPT in general earlier, it’s worth noting that in the academic context, it’s free for essential use, which has led to broad adoption among students. The ChatGPT Plus ($20/mo) is often used by researchers who need the more advanced GPT-4 model for better accuracy in technical topics or need access even during peak times. 雖然我們之前已經討論過 ChatGPT 的一般用途，但值得一提的是，在學術環境中，它對基本用途是免費的，這使得學生廣泛採用。ChatGPT Plus（$20/月）則常被研究者使用，他們需要更先進的 GPT-4 模型以提高技術主題的準確性，或是在高峰時間仍能使用。

    OpenAI also offers GPT-4 API (at ~$ $0.03/1K tokens for input and $0.06/1K output), which some academic developers use to build custom research assistant tools. OpenAI has even announced a ChatGPT Education Pilot (ChatGPT Edu) for campuses with discounted rates​. So, while not an academic-specific tool, ChatGPT is de facto an important AI tool in education. OpenAI 也提供 GPT-4 API（輸入約$0.03/1K tokens，輸出約$0.06/1K tokens），有些學術開發者會用來建立自訂的研究助理工具。OpenAI 甚至宣布了一個 ChatGPT 教育試點計畫（ChatGPT Edu），為校園提供折扣價格。因此，雖然 ChatGPT 不是專為學術設計的工具，但它已成為教育領域事實上的重要 AI 工具。

    Khanmigo (Khan Academy) –  An AI tutor integrated into Khan Academy’s platform, powered by GPT-4. Khanmigo can be a student tutor (answering questions step-by-step without giving away the answer, guiding learning) or an educator teaching assistant (helping draft lesson plans or create quizzes). Khanmigo（Khan Academy）– 一個整合於 Khan Academy 平台的 AI 導師，由 GPT-4 驅動。Khanmigo 可以作為學生導師（逐步回答問題而不直接透露答案，引導學習）或教育者教學助理（協助擬定課程計畫或建立測驗）。

    Use cases: Students stuck on a math problem can ask Khanmigo for help, and Khanmigo will try to coach them to the solution with hints. It can also role-play as characters for learning (e.g., a historical figure for a student to interview in history class). Pricing/ 使用情境：學生卡在數學問題上時，可以向 Khanmigo 求助，Khanmigo 會嘗試透過提示引導學生找到解答。它也可以扮演角色來促進學習（例如，在歷史課上扮演歷史人物，讓學生進行訪問）。

    Availability: Currently, Khanmigo is in a pilot phase—available to a limited number of users. Initially, access was given to donors who contribute $20/month to Khan Academy, but Khan Academy recently announced that Khanmigo will open up more broadly at around $4/month for individuals (and free for certain school district partnerships)​. 可用性：目前，Khanmigo 處於試點階段，僅對有限的用戶開放。最初，只有每月捐贈 20 美元支持 Khan Academy 的捐助者才能使用，但 Khan Academy 最近宣布，Khanmigo 將在約每月 4 美元的費用下對個人用戶更廣泛開放（並對某些學區合作關係提供免費）。

    It’s not yet freely available because they monitor and improve it. The low price indicates Khan Academy’s nonprofit approach to making AI tutoring affordable at scale once it is fully launched. 它尚未完全免費，因為他們持續監測並改進這項服務。低廉的價格顯示 Khan Academy 以非營利方式推動 AI 導師，使其在全面推出後能大規模提供經濟實惠的學習輔導。

    Quizlet (Q-Chat)— Quizlet, a popular study flashcard app, has integrated an AI tutor called Q-Chat. Q-Chat uses ChatGPT’s API to create an interactive tutor who quizzes the student based on Quizlet co ntent. Quizlet (Q-Chat)— Quizlet 是一款廣受歡迎的學習閃卡應用程式，已整合了一個名為 Q-Chat 的 AI 教學助手。Q-Chat 使用 ChatGPT 的 API 來建立一個互動式教學者，根據 Quizlet 的內容對學生進行測試。

    For example, suppose you have a set of flashcards on Spanish vocabulary. In that case, Q-Chat will have a back-and-forth conversation in Spanish, ask you to translate words, and give feedback – essentially turning static flashcards into a dynamic quiz game​. 例如，假設你有一組西班牙語單字的閃卡，Q-Chat 就會以西班牙語進行來回對話，請你翻譯單字並給予反饋—基本上將靜態的閃卡轉化為動態的測驗遊戲。

    It follows a Socratic method by asking questions rather than just letting you flip flashcards​. Pricing: Quizlet is free with ads and flashcards for essential use. Q-Chat, however, is a premium feature requiring Quizlet Plus (approximately $35 per year for students). 它採用蘇格拉底方法，透過提問來引導學習，而非只是讓你翻轉閃卡。

    Quizlet Plus removes ads and adds features like advanced learning modes – Q-Chat is included for subscribers. 價格：Quizlet 提供免費版本，含廣告和基本的閃卡功能。然而 Q-Chat 是高階功能，需要訂閱 Quizlet Plus（學生大約每年 35 美元）。

    Since Q-Chat launched in beta in 2023, Quizlet Plus subscribers have had access to iOS (with expansion to all platforms). There’s no separate charge for Q-Chat beyond the Plus subscription. 自 2023 年 Q-Chat 進入測試版以來，Quizlet Plus 訂閱者已可使用 iOS（後擴展至所有平台）。除了 Plus 訂閱費外，Q-Chat 不另外收取費用。

    Turnitin Originality (AI writing detection) – For academic integrity, it’s worth mentioning Turnitin’s AI writing detection, which many universities are using to check if student essays are AI-generated. This isn’t a tool that helps you create or study; instead, it’s an AI tool that instructors use. Turnitin Originality（AI 寫作檢測）－為維護學術誠信，值得一提的是 Turnitin 的 AI 寫作檢測功能，許多大學正用來檢查學生論文是否為 AI 生成。這不是幫助你學習或創作的工具，而是教師用來檢測的 AI 工具。

    Turnitin claims it can detect GPT-generated text with a certain confidence. It’s bundled in Turnitin’s plagiarism suite for institutions (pricing part of Turnitin license, not sold to individuals). Turnitin 聲稱可以以一定程度的確定性檢測 GPT 生成的文本。此功能包含在 Turnitin 的抄襲檢測套件中，用於機構（價格為 Turnitin 授權的一部分，不對個人銷售）。

    It illustrates the ecosystem: as students use AI like ChatGPT, educators use AI to detect potential misuse. 這說明了生態系統：當學生使用 AI 如 ChatGPT 時，教育者則使用 AI 來檢測潛在的濫用情況。

    Jupyter Notebooks + AI—Jupyter is the classic tool  for coding and analysis in research. Now, tools like Jupyter AI (an extension) allow using LLMs within notebooks, e.g., a magic command to explain code or generate code cells from instructions. Jupyter Notebooks + AI—Jupyter 是研究中編碼與分析的經典工具。現在，像 Jupyter AI（一個擴充套件）這樣的工具允許在筆記本中使用 LLMs，例如，透過魔術指令來解釋程式碼或根據指示產生程式碼區塊。

    This is experimental but shows up in academia, where data science students can get AI help directly in the environment they code. It’s open source and free (requires hooking to an API like OpenAI or local model). 這屬於實驗性質，但在學術界已出現，數據科學學生可以在他們編碼的環境中直接獲得 AI 的協助。它是開源且免費的（需要連結到像 OpenAI 或本地模型這樣的 API）。

    (Academic researchers also heavily use open-source AI frameworks (next section) to develop new AI models, but those are more about creating AI than using AI to assist in general tasks. Regarding widely available tools for academic assignments, the above covers literature review, studying, and tutoring.) （學術研究者也大量使用開源 AI 框架（下一節）來開發新的 AI 模型，但這些更多是關於建立 AI 而非用 AI 來協助一般任務。關於廣泛可用的學術作業工具，上述內容涵蓋了文獻回顧、學習與輔導。）

    AI Development Frameworks and Open-Source Libraries AI 開發框架與開源函式庫

    For those building AI models (in business R&D or academic research), some key frameworks and tools are widely used and freely available: 

    TensorFlow – An open-source deep learning framework initially developed by Google. TensorFlow allows constructing neural networks (from simple to very large) and computation on GPUs/TPUs for acceleration. It’s used in research and production (vision, NLP, etc.).  

    Features: It supports high-level APIs like Keras for ease of use and lower-level ops for custom model building. It has a rich ecosystem (TensorBoard for visualization, TensorFlow Lite for mobile, etc.).  

    Pricing:  TensorFlow is entirely free and open-source (Apache 2.0 license). It requires computing resources—which one might pay for in the cloud or invest in GPUs—but the software is inexpensive. It’s heavily used in academia (many ML courses use TensorFlow/Keras) and industry (Google uses it internally, and others use it in products). 

    PyTorch – Another open-source deep learning library, initially by Facebook (Meta). PyTorch has become very popular in research due to its dynamic computation graph (which feels more like regular Python code) and intuitive API. It’s widely used in cutting-edge AI developments (most NLP breakthrough models, like transformers, were first implemented in PyTorch). Features: strong support for GPU acceleration, a large set of built-in neural network layers and loss functions, and a growing ecosystem (e.g., PyTorch Lightning for easier training loops).
